namespace = DR_cults


# openly_adopt_faith - Convert cultists
character_event = {
	id = DR_cults.3800
	desc = EVTDESC_DR_CULTS_3800
    picture = GFX_evt_society_joining
    border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		set_character_flag = currently_part_of_secret_religion_uncovering
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_DR_CULTS_3800
		convert_to_secret_religion = yes
		leave_society = yes
		#set_defacto_liege = event_target:cultist_leader_revolting
		#set_character_flag = independent_joining_flag
        if = {
            limit = { ai = yes }
            set_character_flag = ai_flag_refuse_conversion
        }
		if = {
			limit = {
				higher_tier_than = BARON
				AND = {
					liege = {
						NOT = { secret_religion_group = chaos_gods_group }
						independent = yes
					}
				}
			}
			liege = {
				ROOT = {
					set_defacto_liege = PREV
				}
				reverse_war = {
					target = ROOT
					casus_belli = cultist_bid_for_independence
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				higher_tier_than = BARON
				AND = {
					liege = {
						liege = {
							NOT = { secret_religion_group = chaos_gods_group }
							independent = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			liege = {
				liege = {
					ROOT = {
						set_defacto_liege = PREV
					}
					reverse_war = {
						target = ROOT
						casus_belli = cultist_bid_for_independence
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

character_event = { # Openly Adopt Faith event (for the character who actually fires all of it)
    id = DR_cults.3811
    desc = EVTDESC_DR_CULTS_3811
    picture = GFX_evt_dark_prayer
    border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
    is_triggered_only = yes

    option = {
        name = EVTOPTA_DR_CULTS_3811
        custom_tooltip = { text = EVTOPTA_DR_CULTS_3811_TT }
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = devout_leader
			duration = -1
		}
		save_event_target_as = cultist_leader_revolting
			if = {
				limit = {
				top_liege = {
					NOR = {
						same_society_as = event_target:cultist_leader_revolting
						secret_religion = chaos_gods_group
		}
				}
			}
			top_liege = {
				ROOT = {
					set_defacto_liege = PREV
				}
				save_event_target_as = top_liege_defending
				reverse_war = {
					target = ROOT
					casus_belli = cultist_bid_for_independence
				}
			}
			event_target:top_liege_defending = {
				any_realm_character = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								same_society_as = event_target:cultist_leader_revolting
								secret_religion_group = chaos_gods_group
							}
						}
						character_event = { id = DR_cults.3800 } # Convert cultists
					}
				}
			}
		}

        if = {
            limit = { ai = yes }
            set_character_flag = ai_flag_refuse_conversion
        }
    }
}


# openly_adopt_faith - Flip provinces with local cult modifier
character_event = {
	id = DR_cults.3820
	desc = EVTDESC_DR_CULTS_3820
    picture = GFX_evt_society_joining
    border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_DR_CULTS_3820
		FROM = {
			flip_secret_religious_community_provinces = yes
		}
	}
}

    border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion

	is_triggered_only = yes

		NOT = { has_character_flag = currently_part_of_secret_religion_uncovering }
	}

		name = EVTOPTA_DR_CULTS_3830
	}
}

# prepare_grounds - safety flag clear
character_event = {
	id = DR_cults.3849
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		clr_character_flag = preparing_grounds_in_@FROM
	}
}

# prepare_grounds - Start progress
character_event = {
	id = DR_cults.3850
	desc = EVTDESC_DR_CULTS_3850
	picture = GFX_evt_secret_ceremony
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_DR_CULTS_3850
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = EVTTOOLTIP_DR_CULTS_3850
			hidden_effect = {
				random_list = {
					20 = {
						modifier = {
							factor = 0.1
							event_target:target_province = {
								county = {
									holder_scope = {
										NOT = {
											character = ROOT
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
						modifier = {
							factor = 1.1
							diplomacy = 12
						}
						modifier = {
							factor = 1.1
							diplomacy = 14
						}
						modifier = {
							factor = 1.1
							diplomacy = 16
						}
						modifier = {
							factor = 1.1
							diplomacy = 18
						}
						modifier = {
							factor = 1.1
							diplomacy = 20
						}

						if = {
							limit = {
								event_target:target_province = {
									county = {
										holder_scope = {
											NOT = {
												character = ROOT
											}
										}
									}
								}
							}
							character_event = { id = DR_cults.3860 days = 500 random = 50 }
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								event_target:target_province = {
									county = {
										holder_scope = {
											character = ROOT
										}
									}
								}
							}
							character_event = { id = DR_cults.3860 days = 300 random = 50 }
						}
					}
					50 = {
						modifier = {
							factor = 0.2
							event_target:target_province = {
								county = {
									holder_scope = {
										NOT = {
											character = ROOT
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
						modifier = {
							factor = 1.1
							diplomacy = 12
						}
						modifier = {
							factor = 1.1
							diplomacy = 14
						}
						modifier = {
							factor = 1.1
							diplomacy = 16
						}

							factor = 1.1
							diplomacy = 18
						}

							factor = 1.1
							diplomacy = 20

						if = {
							limit = {

									county = {

											NOT = {
												character = ROOT
											}
										}
									}
								}
							}
							character_event = { id = DR_cults.3870 days = 500 random = 50 }
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								event_target:target_province = {
									county = {
										holder_scope = {
											character = ROOT
										}
									}
								}
							}
							character_event = { id = DR_cults.3870 days = 300 random = 50 }
						}
					}
					30 = {
						if = {
							limit = {
								event_target:target_province = {
									county = {
										holder_scope = {
											NOT = {
												character = ROOT
											}
										}
									}
								}
							}
							character_event = { id = DR_cults.3880 days = 500 random = 50 }

									county = {

										}
									}

}

character_event = {
	id = DR_cults.3858
	desc = EVTDESC_DR_CULTS_3858
	picture = GFX_evt_secret_ceremony
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_DR_CULTS_3858
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_quest = quest_chaos_cult_prepare_grounds
				event_target:target_province = {
					is_quest_target_of = ROOT
				}
			}
			clr_quest = { id = quest_chaos_cult_prepare_grounds failure = yes }
		}
		clear_delayed_event = { id = DR_cults.3849 }
		clear_delayed_event = { id = DR_cults.3859 }
		clr_character_flag = preparing_grounds_in_@target_province
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = DR_cults.3859
	hide_window = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				#OR = {
				#	NOT = {
				#		society = {
				#			event_target:original_society = {
				#				society_type = PREV
				#			}
				#		}
				#	}
					event_target:target_province = {
						county = {
							holder_scope = {
								NOT = {
									same_realm = ROOT
								}
							}
						}
					}
				#}
			}
			clear_delayed_event = { id = DR_cults.3860 }
			clear_delayed_event = { id = DR_cults.3870 }
			clear_delayed_event = { id = DR_cults.3880 }
			clear_delayed_event = { id = DR_cults.3890 }
			character_event = { id = DR_cults.3858 }
			break = yes
		}
		repeat_event = { id = DR_cults.3859 days = 30 }
	}
}

character_event = {

		}

		}
	}

		name = EVTOPTB_DR_CULTS_3880
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_quest = quest_chaos_cult_prepare_grounds
				event_target:target_province = {
					is_quest_target_of = ROOT
				}
			}
			clr_quest = { id = quest_chaos_cult_prepare_grounds failure = yes }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			clear_delayed_event = { id = DR_cults.3859 }
			clear_delayed_event = { id = DR_cults.3849 }
			clr_character_flag = preparing_grounds_in_@target_province
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = DR_cults.3890
	desc = EVTDESC_DR_CULTS_3890
	picture = GFX_evt_secret_ceremony
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_DR_CULTS_3890
		trigger_switch = {
			on_trigger = society_member_of
			cult_of_khorne = {
				event_target:target_province = {
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = secret_khorne_community
						duration = -1
					}
				}
			}
			cult_of_nurgle = {
				event_target:target_province = {
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = secret_nurgle_community
						duration = -1
					}
				}
			}
			cult_of_tzeentch = {
				event_target:target_province = {
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = secret_tzeentch_community
						duration = -1
					}
				}
			}
			cult_of_slaanesh = {
				event_target:target_province = {
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = secret_slaanesh_community
						duration = -1
					}
				}
			}
			cult_of_undivided = {
				event_target:target_province = {
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = secret_undivided_community
						duration = -1
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_quest = quest_chaos_cult_prepare_grounds
				event_target:target_province = {
					is_quest_target_of = ROOT
				}
			}
			clr_quest = quest_chaos_cult_prepare_grounds

			add_society_currency_minor_effect = yes
		}
		clear_delayed_event = { id = DR_cults.3849 }
		clr_character_flag = preparing_grounds_in_@target_province

		hidden_effect = {
			clear_delayed_event = { id = DR_cults.3859 }
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = DR_cults.3900
	hide_window = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		FROM = { society_quest_event = { id = DR_cults.3901 days = 7 random = 7 } }
	}
}

society_quest_event = {
	id = DR_cults.3901
    border = GFX_event_letter_frame_religion

    desc = EVTDESC_DR_CULTS_3901

    is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		random_demesne_province = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
                    AND = {
                        ROOT = { society_member_of = cult_of_khorne }
                        NOR = {
                            religion = khorne
                            has_province_modifier = secret_khorne_community
                        }
                    }
                    AND = {
                        ROOT = { society_member_of = cult_of_nurgle }
                        NOR = {
                            religion = khorne
                            has_province_modifier = secret_nurgle_community
                        }
                    }
                    AND = {
                        ROOT = { society_member_of = cult_of_tzeentch }
                        NOR = {
                            religion = khorne
                            has_province_modifier = secret_tzeentch_community
                        }
                    }
                    AND = {
                        ROOT = { society_member_of = cult_of_slaanesh }
                        NOR = {
                            religion = khorne
                            has_province_modifier = secret_slaanesh_community
                        }
                    }
                    AND = {
                        ROOT = { society_member_of = cult_of_undivided }
                        NOR = {
                            religion = khorne
                            has_province_modifier = secret_undivided_community
                        }
                    }
                }
			}
			save_event_target_as = target_province
		}
	}

    option = {
        name = ACCEPT
		event_target:target_province = {
			set_quest_target = {
				id = quest_chaos_cult_prepare_grounds
				holder = ROOT
			}
		}
    }

    option = {
        name = DECLINE
        custom_tooltip = { text = decline_quest_tooltip }

        add_character_modifier = {
            name = quest_cooldown_timer
            hidden = yes
            days = 1000
        }

        ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
    }
}

### minor/major soul corruption effect (on yearly pulse)
character_event = {
	id = DR_cults.7000

	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		is_devil_worshiper_trigger = yes
		days_in_society > 1095
		has_dlc = Mystics
	}

	immediate = {
		random_list = { #randomizes between big or small effect, both containing a chance of nothing happening
			50 = {
				minor_chaos_corruption_effect = yes
			}
			50 = {
				minor_chaos_corruption_effect = yes
			}
		}
	}
}


###JOINING & RECRUITMENT EVENTS###

#For the recruit: Do you approve of "alternative views"?
character_event = {
	id = DR_cults.7001
	desc = EVTDESC_DR_CULTS_7001_A
	picture = GFX_evt_shady_meeting
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = { has_dlc = Mystics }

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { event_target:chaos_cult_recruiter = { always = yes } } }
			FROMFROM = { save_event_target_as = chaos_cult_recruiter }
		}
		save_event_target_as = chaos_cult_recruit
	}

	#Approving of heretics
	option = {
		name = {
			text = EVTOPTA_7001 #If God didn't want us to ask questions, why did he make us curious?
		}

		trigger = {
			OR = {
				ai = no
				NOT = { controls_religion = yes }
			}
		}

		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTOPTA_7001_TT }

		reverse_opinion = {
			who = event_target:chaos_cult_recruiter
			modifier = opinion_agreed_with_opinion
			years = 5
		}

		set_character_flag = approves_of_satanism

		hidden_effect = {
			character_event = { id = DR_cults.6999 days = 3 }
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				trait = zealous
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = trusting
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				is_dumb_trigger = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_khorne
				is_strong_trigger = yes
			}


			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = ambitious
				has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_tzeentch
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = deceitful
				has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_tzeentch

			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				is_smart_trigger = yes
				has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_tzeentch
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				is_ill = yes
				has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_nurgle
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = content
				has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_nurgle

			}


			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_slaanesh
				trait = hedonist
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_slaanesh
				trait = lustful
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = cynical
			}
		}
	}

	#Disapproving of heretics
	option = {
		name = {
			text = EVTOPTB_7001
		}

		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTOPTB_7001_TT }

		reverse_opinion = {
			who = event_target:chaos_cult_recruiter
			modifier = opinion_disagreed_with_opinion
			years = 5
		}

		set_character_flag = disapproves_of_satanism

		clr_character_flag = being_recruited_by_khorne
		clr_character_flag = being_recruited_by_nurgle
		clr_character_flag = being_recruited_by_tzeentch
		clr_character_flag = being_recruited_by_slaanesh
		clr_character_flag = being_recruited_by_undivided

		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:chaos_cult_recruiter = {
				character_event = { id = DR_cults.7002 days = 15 }
			}
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				has_pious_trait_trigger = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				has_crusade_trait_trigger = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

# Safety ping.
character_event = {
	id = DR_cults.6999
	hide_window = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:chaos_cult_recruiter = {
					is_alive = yes
					is_devil_worshiper_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			event_target:chaos_cult_recruiter = {
				character_event = { id = DR_cults.7002 }
			}
			break = yes
		}
		# Else notify broken chain
		character_event = { id = DR_cults.6995 }
	}
}

# Safety ping.
character_event = {
	id = DR_cults.6996
	hide_window = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:chaos_cult_recruiter = {
					is_alive = yes
					is_devil_worshiper_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			event_target:chaos_cult_recruiter = {
				character_event = { id = DR_cults.7006 }
			}
			break = yes
		}
		# Else notify broken chain
		character_event = { id = DR_cults.6995 }
	}
}

	immediate = {

				factor = 1.1
				has_lifestyle_intrigue_trigger = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.1
				trait = trusting
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				is_dumb_trigger = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_khorne
				is_strong_trigger = yes
			}


			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5

				trait = cynical

			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5

			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				FROM = { intrigue = 12 }
			}
			modifier = {

				FROM = { trait = fair }

		clr_character_flag = being_recruited_by_nurgle
		clr_character_flag = being_recruited_by_tzeentch
		clr_character_flag = being_recruited_by_slaanesh

character_event = {
	id = DR_cults.7005

	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	desc = EVTDESC_DR_CULTS_7005

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { any_lover = { has_disease_trigger = yes } }
				set_character_flag = has_ill_lover_loc
			}
			if = {
				limit = { any_spouse = { has_disease_trigger = yes }}
				set_character_flag = has_ill_spouse_loc
			}
			if = {
				limit = { any_child = { has_disease_trigger = yes }	}
				set_character_flag = has_ill_child_loc
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { wealth = 0 } }
				set_character_flag = has_money_troubles_loc
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { wealth = 0 } }
				set_character_flag = has_money_troubles_loc
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_disease_trigger = yes }
				set_character_flag = has_some_illness_loc
			}
			if = {
				limit = { war = yes	}
				set_character_flag = has_need_of_winning_battles_loc
			}
			if = {
				limit = { any_rival = { always = yes } }
				set_character_flag = has_a_rival_loc
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						trait = weak
						trait = feeble
						trait = dwarf
						trait = hunchback
					}
				}
				set_character_flag = is_weak_loc
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						trait = imbecile
						trait = inbred
						trait = slow
					}
				}
				set_character_flag = is_dumb_loc
			}
		}
	}

	#Yes - can you help me [GetDWReasonToJoin]?
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_7005
		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTOPTA_7005_TT }

		hidden_effect = { character_event = { id = DR_cults.6997 days = 5 } }

	}

	#No - this is blasphemy, get out of my sight

		name = EVTOPTB_7005
		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTOPTB_7005_TT }
		clr_character_flag = being_recruited_by_khorne
		clr_character_flag = being_recruited_by_nurgle
		clr_character_flag = being_recruited_by_tzeentch
		clr_character_flag = being_recruited_by_slaanesh

		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}

#"Await the messenger" a letter reads
letter_event = {
	id = DR_cults.7014
	desc = EVTDESC_DR_CULTS_7014
	border = GFX_event_letter_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_7014
		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTOPTA_7014_TT }

		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:chaos_cult_inductor = {
				clr_character_flag = event_DR_CULTS_7014
			}

			#KHORNE
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_khorne
					any_society_member = {
						society_member_of = cult_of_khorne
						is_strong_trigger = yes
					}
				}
				random_society_member = {
					limit = {
						society_member_of = cult_of_khorne
						is_strong_trigger = yes
					}
					save_event_target_as = chaos_cult_inductor
					set_character_flag = event_DR_CULTS_7015
					character_event = { id = DR_cults.7013 }
					break = yes
				}
			}

			#NURGLE
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_nurgle
					any_society_member = {
						society_member_of = cult_of_nurgle
						is_ill = yes
					}
				}
				random_society_member = {
					limit = {
						society_member_of = cult_of_nurgle
						is_ill = yes
					}
					save_event_target_as = chaos_cult_inductor
					set_character_flag = event_DR_CULTS_7015
					character_event = { id = DR_cults.7013 }
					break = yes
				}
			}

			#TZEENTCH
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_tzeentch
					any_society_member = {
						society_member_of = cult_of_tzeentch
						is_mutated_trigger = yes
					}
				}
				random_society_member = {
					limit = {
						society_member_of = cult_of_tzeentch
						is_mutated_trigger = yes
					}
					save_event_target_as = chaos_cult_inductor
					set_character_flag = event_DR_CULTS_7015
					character_event = { id = DR_cults.7013 }
					break = yes
				}
			}

			#SLAANESH
			if = {
				limit = {
					prefers_men_trigger = yes
					has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_slaanesh
					any_society_member = {
						society_member_of = cult_of_slaanesh
						is_female = no
						is_attractive_trigger = yes
					}
				}
				random_society_member = {
					limit = {
						society_member_of = cult_of_slaanesh
						is_female = no
						is_attractive_trigger = yes
					}
					save_event_target_as = chaos_cult_inductor
					set_character_flag = event_DR_CULTS_7015
					character_event = { id = DR_cults.7013 }
					break = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					prefers_men_trigger = no
					has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_slaanesh
					any_society_member = {
						society_member_of = cult_of_slaanesh
						is_female = yes
						is_attractive_trigger = yes
					}
				}
				random_society_member = {
					limit = {
						society_member_of = cult_of_slaanesh
						is_female = yes
						is_attractive_trigger = yes
					}
					save_event_target_as = chaos_cult_inductor
					set_character_flag = event_DR_CULTS_7015
					character_event = { id = DR_cults.7013 }
					break = yes
				}
			}

			#UNDIVIDED
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_undivided
				}
				random_society_member = {
					limit = {
						society_member_of = cult_of_undivided
					}
					save_event_target_as = chaos_cult_inductor
					set_character_flag = event_DR_CULTS_7015
					character_event = { id = DR_cults.7013 }
					break = yes
				}
			}



			if = { #back up if there is no eligble society member
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_khorne
						has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_nurgle
						has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_tzeentch
						has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_undivided
					}
				}
				create_character = {
					random_traits = yes
					dynasty = none
					religion = ROOT
					culture = ROOT
					female = no
					age = 20
					attributes = {
						intrigue = 5
					}
					historical = yes
				}
				new_character = {
					# Set Racial Trait
					character_event = {
					  id = aiclean.31
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							ROOT = { has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_khorne }
						}
						add_trait = strong
						add_trait = skilled_tactician
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							ROOT = { has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_nurgle}
						}
						add_trait = pneumonic
						nurgle_blessing_check_effect = yes
						add_trait = fortune_builder
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							ROOT = { has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_tzeentch }
						}
						add_trait = beak
						add_trait = elusive_shadow
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							ROOT = { has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_undivided }
						}
						add_trait = beak
						add_trait = scholarly_theologian
					}
					save_event_target_as = chaos_cult_inductor
					set_character_flag = event_DR_CULTS_7015
					ROOT = {
						trigger_switch = {
							on_trigger = has_character_flag
							being_recruited_by_khorne = { PREV = { join_society = cult_of_khorne set_secret_religion = khorne } }
							being_recruited_by_nurgle = { PREV = { join_society = cult_of_nurgle set_secret_religion = nurgle } }
							being_recruited_by_tzeentch = { PREV = { join_society = cult_of_tzeentch set_secret_religion = tzeentch } }
							being_recruited_by_slaanesh = { PREV = { join_society = cult_of_slaanesh set_secret_religion = slaanesh } }
							being_recruited_by_undivided = { PREV = { join_society = cult_of_undivided set_secret_religion = chaos } }
						}
					}
					character_event = { id = DR_cults.7013 }
				}
			}

			if = { #back up if there is no eligble society member
				limit = {
					has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_slaanesh
					prefers_men_trigger = yes
				}
				create_character = {
					random_traits = yes
					dynasty = none
					religion = ROOT
					culture = ROOT
					female = no
					age = 20
					attributes = {
						intrigue = 5
					}
					trait = elusive_shadow
					historical = yes
				}
				new_character = {
					# Set Racial Trait
					character_event = {
					  id = aiclean.31
					}
					remove_trait = ugly
					remove_trait = hunchback
					remove_trait = dwarf
					remove_trait = chaste
					add_trait = lustful
					add_trait = fair
					save_event_target_as = chaos_cult_inductor
					set_character_flag = event_DR_CULTS_7015
					ROOT = {
						trigger_switch = {
							on_trigger = has_character_flag
							being_recruited_by_khorne = { PREV = { join_society = cult_of_khorne set_secret_religion = khorne } }
							being_recruited_by_nurgle = { PREV = { join_society = cult_of_nurgle set_secret_religion = nurgle } }
							being_recruited_by_tzeentch = { PREV = { join_society = cult_of_tzeentch set_secret_religion = tzeentch } }
							being_recruited_by_slaanesh = { PREV = { join_society = cult_of_slaanesh set_secret_religion = slaanesh } }
							being_recruited_by_undivided = { PREV = { join_society = cult_of_undivided set_secret_religion = chaos } }
						}
					}
					character_event = { id = DR_cults.7013 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_slaanesh
					prefers_men_trigger = no
				}
				create_character = {
					random_traits = yes
					dynasty = none
					religion = ROOT
					culture = ROOT
					female = yes
					age = 20
					attributes = {
						intrigue = 5
					}
					trait = elusive_shadow
					historical = yes
				}
				new_character = {
					# Set Racial Trait
					character_event = {
					  id = aiclean.31
					}
					remove_trait = ugly
					remove_trait = hunchback
					remove_trait = dwarf
					remove_trait = chaste
					add_trait = lustful
					add_trait = fair
					save_event_target_as = chaos_cult_inductor
					set_character_flag = event_DR_CULTS_7015
					ROOT = {
						trigger_switch = {
							on_trigger = has_character_flag
							being_recruited_by_khorne = { PREV = { join_society = cult_of_khorne set_secret_religion = khorne } }
							being_recruited_by_nurgle = { PREV = { join_society = cult_of_nurgle set_secret_religion = nurgle } }
							being_recruited_by_tzeentch = { PREV = { join_society = cult_of_tzeentch set_secret_religion = tzeentch } }
							being_recruited_by_slaanesh = { PREV = { join_society = cult_of_slaanesh set_secret_religion = slaanesh } }
							being_recruited_by_undivided = { PREV = { join_society = cult_of_undivided set_secret_religion = chaos } }
						}
					}
					character_event = { id = DR_cults.7013 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Safety ping
character_event = {
	id = DR_cults.6994
	hide_window = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:chaos_cult_inductor = { is_alive = yes }
			}
			event_target:chaos_cult_inductor = {
				clr_character_flag = event_DR_CULTS_7015
				set_character_flag = event_DR_CULTS_7016
				character_event = { id = DR_cults.7013 }
			}
			break = yes
		}
		# Else notify failure
		character_event = { id = DR_cults.6993 }
	}
}

# Prove your ambition
character_event = {
	id = DR_cults.7017
	picture = GFX_evt_secret_ceremony
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_khorne
			event_target:khornate_sacrifice = { always = yes }
		}
		text = EVTDESC_DR_CULTS_7017_A1
	}

	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_khorne
			NOT = { event_target:khornate_sacrifice = { always = yes } }
		}
		text = EVTDESC_DR_CULTS_7017_A2
	}

	desc = {
		trigger = { has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_nurgle }
		text = EVTDESC_DR_CULTS_7017_B
	}

	desc = {
		trigger = { has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_tzeentch }
		text = EVTDESC_DR_CULTS_7017_C
	}

	desc = {
		trigger = { has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_slaanesh }
		text = EVTDESC_DR_CULTS_7017_D
	}

	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_undivided
			event_target:undivided_sacrifice = { always = yes }
		}
		text = EVTDESC_DR_CULTS_7017_E1
	}

	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_undivided
			NOT = { event_target:undivided_sacrifice = { always = yes } }
		}
		text = EVTDESC_DR_CULTS_7017_E2
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_khorne
			}

			random_courtier_or_vassal = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { society_member_of = cult_of_khorne }
					trait = weak
					is_adult = yes
					ai = yes
				}
				save_event_target_as = khornate_sacrifice
			}
			random_courtier_or_vassal = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { society_member_of = cult_of_khorne }
					trait = feeble
					is_adult = yes
					ai = yes
				}
				save_event_target_as = khornate_sacrifice
			}
			random_courtier_or_vassal = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { society_member_of = cult_of_khorne }
					trait = craven
					is_adult = yes
					ai = yes
				}
				save_event_target_as = khornate_sacrifice
			}
			random_courtier_or_vassal = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { society_member_of = cult_of_khorne }
					is_primary_heir = no
					OR = {
						is_lover = ROOT
						is_friend = ROOT
						is_close_relative = ROOT
					}
					is_adult = yes
					ai = yes
				}
				save_event_target_as = khornate_sacrifice
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_undivided
			}

			random_courtier_or_vassal = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { society_member_of = cult_of_undivided }
					is_theocracy = yes
					is_adult = yes
					ai = yes
				}
				save_event_target_as = undivided_sacrifice
			}
			random_courtier_or_vassal = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { society_member_of = cult_of_undivided }
					is_priest = yes
					ai = yes
				}
				save_event_target_as = undivided_sacrifice
			}
		}
	}

	#Anything for the coven and the power you offer
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_7017_DR


		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_khorne
				event_target:khornate_sacrifice = { always = yes }
			}
			custom_tooltip = { text = EVTOPTA_7017_TT_A }
			event_target:khornate_sacrifice = {
				if = {
				  limit = { is_invincible_trigger = yes }
				  antideath_effect = yes
				  break = yes
				}
				death = { death_reason = death_murder_unknown killer = ROOT }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_khorne
				NOT = { event_target:khornate_sacrifice = { always = yes } }
			}
			custom_tooltip = { text = EVTOPTA_7017_TT_A }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_nurgle
			}
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = EVTOPTA_7017_TT_B
					hidden_tooltip = {
						random_list = {
							6 = {
								give_pneumonic_effect = yes
							}
							6 = {
								give_has_tuberculosis_effect = yes
							}
							6 = {
								give_has_typhoid_fever_effect = yes
							}
							6 = {
								give_has_bubonic_plague_effect = yes
							}
							6 = {
								give_has_measles_effect = yes
							}
							6 = {
								give_has_small_pox_effect = yes
							}
							6 = {
								give_has_aztec_disease_effect = yes
							}
							6 = {
								give_syphilitic_effect = yes
							}
							6 = {
								give_flu_effect = yes
							}
							6 = {
								give_dysentery_effect = yes
							}
							6 = {
								give_gout_effect = yes
							}
							6 = {
								give_food_poisoning_effect = yes
							}
							6 = {
								give_rabies_effect = yes
							}
							6 = {
								give_cancer_effect = yes
							}
							6 = {
								give_ill_effect = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}


		}


		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_tzeentch
			}
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = EVTOPTA_7017_TT_C
					hidden_tooltip = {
						mutations_table_tzeentch = yes
					}
				}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_slaanesh
			}

			custom_tooltip = { text = EVTOPTA_7017_TT_D }
		}


		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_undivided
				event_target:undivided_sacrifice = { always = yes }
			}
			event_target:undivided_sacrifice = {
				if = {
				  limit = { is_invincible_trigger = yes }
				  antideath_effect = yes
				  break = yes
				}
				death = { death_reason = death_murder_unknown killer = ROOT } }
			custom_tooltip = { text = EVTOPTA_7017_TT_E }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_undivided
				NOT = { event_target:undivided_sacrifice = { always = yes } }
			}
			custom_tooltip = { text = EVTOPTA_7017_TT_E }
		}


		hidden_effect = {
			character_event = { id = DR_cults.6989 }
		}

		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	}

	#I... I can't do this!
	option = {
		name = {
			text = EVTOPTB_7017
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_khorne
					has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_nurgle
					has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_tzeentch
					has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_undivided
					AND = {
						is_married = no
						has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_slaanesh
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = {
			text = EVTOPTC_7017
			trigger = {
				is_married = yes
				has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_slaanesh
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTOPTB_7017_TT }

		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				#Getaway
				33 = {
					set_character_flag = escape_successful

					modifier = {
						factor = 1.4
						attribute_diff = { character = FROM attribute = intrigue value = 2 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.4
						attribute_diff = { character = FROM attribute = intrigue value = 4 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.4
						attribute_diff = { character = FROM attribute = intrigue value = 6 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.4
						combat_rating_diff = { character = FROM value = 1 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.4
						combat_rating_diff = { character = FROM value = 2 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.4
						combat_rating_diff = { character = FROM value = 3 }
					}
				}
				#Injured
				33 = {
					set_character_flag = escape_injured
				}
				#Death
				33 = {
					set_character_flag = escape_death
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.4
						FROM = { attribute_diff = { character = ROOT attribute = intrigue value = 2 } }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.4
						FROM = { attribute_diff = { character = ROOT attribute = intrigue value = 4 } }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.4
						FROM = { attribute_diff = { character = ROOT attribute = intrigue value = 6 } }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.4
						FROM = { combat_rating_diff = { character = ROOT value = 1 } }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.4
						FROM = { combat_rating_diff = { character = ROOT value = 2 } }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.4
						FROM = { combat_rating_diff = { character = ROOT value = 3 } }
					}
				}
			}

			character_event = { id = DR_cults.6988 }
		}

		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}
}

#You are a member! - The inductor sleeping soundly
character_event = {
	id = DR_cults.7018
	picture = GFX_evt_secret_ceremony
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	desc = {
		trigger = { has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_khorne }
		text = EVTDESC_DR_CULTS_7018
	}

	desc = {
		trigger = { has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_nurgle }
		text = EVTDESC_DR_CULTS_7018B
	}

	desc = {
		trigger = { has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_tzeentch }
		text = EVTDESC_DR_CULTS_7018C
	}

	desc = {
		trigger = { has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_slaanesh }
		text = EVTDESC_DR_CULTS_7018D
	}

	desc = {
		trigger = { has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_undivided }
		text = EVTDESC_DR_CULTS_7018E
	}


	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		#If original recruiter is still around, find Grand Master and have them send word of success to that original recruiter
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { event_target:chaos_cult_recruiter = { always = yes } }
				event_target:chaos_cult_recruiter = { set_character_flag = recruitment_success }

				if = { limit = { has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_khorne }
					random_society_member = {
						limit = {
							society_rank = {
								rank == 4
								society = cult_of_khorne
							}
						}
						save_event_target_as = grand_master
					}
				}
				if = { limit = { has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_nurgle }
					random_society_member = {
						limit = {
							society_rank = {
								rank == 4
								society = cult_of_nurgle
							}
						}
						save_event_target_as = grand_master
					}
				}
				if = { limit = { has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_tzeentch }
					random_society_member = {
						limit = {
							society_rank = {
								rank == 4
								society = cult_of_tzeentch
							}
						}
						save_event_target_as = grand_master
					}
				}
				if = { limit = { has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_slaanesh }
					random_society_member = {
						limit = {
							society_rank = {
								rank == 4
								society = cult_of_slaanesh
							}
						}
						save_event_target_as = grand_master
					}
				}
				if = { limit = { has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_undivided}
					random_society_member = {
						limit = {
							society_rank = {
								rank == 4
								society = cult_of_undivided
							}
						}
						save_event_target_as = grand_master
					}
				}
				event_target:grand_master = { character_event = { id = DR_cults.7021 } }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_7018 # I wish you'd found me sooner
		trigger = { has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_slaanesh }

		join_cult_as_member_or_sleeper_agent = yes

		if = {
			limit = { ai = no }
		}

		opinion = {
			who = event_target:chaos_cult_inductor
			modifier = opinion_budding_romance
		}

		event_target:chaos_cult_inductor = {
			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = opinion_budding_friendship
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			clr_character_flag = being_recruited_by_khorne
			clr_character_flag = being_recruited_by_nurgle
			clr_character_flag = being_recruited_by_tzeentch
			clr_character_flag = being_recruited_by_slaanesh
			clr_character_flag = being_recruited_by_undivided
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_7018_DR # this was a necessary evil

		join_cult_as_member_or_sleeper_agent = yes

		# event_target:chaos_cult_inductor = {
			# opinion = {

				# modifier = opinion_very_disappointed
			# }
		# }

			if = {
				limit = { event_target:chaos_cult_recruiter = { always = yes } }
				event_target:chaos_cult_recruiter = { set_character_flag = recruitment_success } #notify original recruiter
				if = { limit = { has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_khorne }
					random_society_member = {
						limit = {
							society_rank = {
								rank == 4
								society = cult_of_khorne
							}
						}
						save_event_target_as = grand_master
					}
				}
				if = { limit = { has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_khorne }
					random_society_member = {
						limit = {
							society_rank = {
								rank == 4
								society = cult_of_khorne
							}
						}
						save_event_target_as = grand_master
					}
				}
				if = { limit = { has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_nurgle }
					random_society_member = {

							society_rank = {
								rank == 4
								society = cult_of_nurgle
							}
						}
						save_event_target_as = grand_master
					}
				}
				if = { limit = { has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_tzeentch }
					random_society_member = {

							society_rank = {

#You flee
character_event = {
	id = DR_cults.7019
	picture = GFX_evt_secret_ceremony
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	desc = {
		trigger = { has_character_flag = escape_successful }
		text = EVTDESC_DR_CULTS_7019_A
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_character_flag = escape_injured }
		text = EVTDESC_DR_CULTS_7019_B
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_character_flag = escape_death }
		text = EVTDESC_DR_CULTS_7019_C
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		#If original recruiter is still around, find Grand Master and have them send word of failure to that original recruiter
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { event_target:chaos_cult_recruiter = { always = yes } }
				event_target:chaos_cult_recruiter = { set_character_flag = recruitment_fail }

				if = { limit = { has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_khorne }
					random_society_member = {
						limit = {
							society_rank = {
								rank == 4
								society = cult_of_khorne
							}
						}
						save_event_target_as = grand_master
					}
				}
				if = { limit = { has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_nurgle }
					random_society_member = {
						limit = {
							society_rank = {
								rank == 4
								society = cult_of_nurgle
							}
						}
						save_event_target_as = grand_master
					}
				}
				if = { limit = { has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_tzeentch }
					random_society_member = {
						limit = {
							society_rank = {
								rank == 4
								society = cult_of_tzeentch
							}
						}
						save_event_target_as = grand_master
					}
				}
				if = { limit = { has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_slaanesh }
					random_society_member = {
						limit = {
							society_rank = {
								rank == 4
								society = cult_of_slaanesh
							}
						}
						save_event_target_as = grand_master
					}
				}
				if = { limit = { has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_undivided }
					random_society_member = {
						limit = {
							society_rank = {
								rank == 4
								society = cult_of_undivided
							}
						}
						save_event_target_as = grand_master
					}
				}
				event_target:grand_master = { character_event = { id = DR_cults.7021 } }
			}
		}

			clr_character_flag = being_recruited_by_khorne
			clr_character_flag = being_recruited_by_nurgle
			clr_character_flag = being_recruited_by_tzeentch
			clr_character_flag = being_recruited_by_slaanesh
			clr_character_flag = being_recruited_by_undivided
	}

	#Escape successfully
	option = {
		trigger = { has_character_flag = escape_successful }
		name = EVTOPTA_7019
		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTOPTA_7019_TT }

		clr_character_flag = escape_successful
	}

	#Escaped but got injured
	option = {
		trigger = { has_character_flag = escape_injured }
		name = EVTOPTB_7019
		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTOPTB_7019_TT }

		clr_character_flag = escape_injured

		add_maimed_trait_effect = yes
	}

	#Escaped but died
	option = {
		trigger = { has_character_flag = escape_death }
		name = EVTOPTC_7019
		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTOPTC_7019_TT }
		if = {
		  limit = { is_invincible_trigger = yes }
		  antideath_effect = yes
		  break = yes
		}
		death = { death_reason = death_murder_unknown killer = FROM }
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = DR_cults.7030
	hide_window = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_khorne
							NOT = { society_member_of = cult_of_khorne }
						}
						AND = {
							has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_nurgle
							NOT = { society_member_of = cult_of_nurgle}
						}
						AND = {
							has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_tzeentch
							NOT = { society_member_of = cult_of_tzeentch }

							has_character_flag = being_recruited_by_undivided
							NOT = { society_member_of = cult_of_undivided }
						}

							has_character_flag = assassins_attempted_recruitment
							NOT = { society_member_of = the_assassins }
						}
						AND = {
							has_character_flag = eshin_attempted_recruitment
							NOT = { society_member_of = eshin_society }
						}
					}
				}

					random_society_member = {

					}

								society = cult_of_nurgle

#Soul Corruption event
character_event = {
	id = DR_cults.7050
	picture = GFX_evt_dark_prayer
	desc = EVTDESC_MNM_7050
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	hide_from = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_MNM_7050
		trigger_switch = {
			on_trigger = has_character_flag
			corruption_remove_kind = {
				remove_trait = kind
				clr_character_flag = corruption_remove_kind
			}
			corruption_add_cruel = {
				add_trait = cruel
				clr_character_flag = corruption_add_cruel
			}
			corruption_remove_just = {
				remove_trait = just
				clr_character_flag = corruption_remove_just
			}
			corruption_add_arbitrary = {
				add_trait = arbitrary
				clr_character_flag = corruption_add_arbitrary
			}
			corruption_remove_honest = {
				remove_trait = honest
				clr_character_flag = corruption_remove_honest
			}
			corruption_add_deceitful = {
				add_trait = deceitful
				clr_character_flag = corruption_add_deceitful
			}
			corruption_add_possessed = {
				add_trait = possessed
				clr_character_flag = corruption_add_possessed
			}
		}
	}
}

#Power: Corrupt a priest

#Ping event for Corrupt a priest
character_event = {
	id = DR_cults.7825
	hide_window = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = corrupt_priest_target
		FROMFROM = {
			save_event_target_as = corrupt_priest_spell_caster
		}
		event_target:corrupt_priest_spell_caster = {
			character_event = { id = DR_cults.7826 }
		}
	}
}

#Corrupt a Priest (find out whether corruptible)
character_event = {
	id = DR_cults.7826
	picture = GFX_evt_dark_prayer
	desc = EVTDESC_MNM_7826
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		is_devil_worshiper_trigger = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_MNM_7826 #try to find something new to corrupt them with (add new sinful traits)
		trigger = {
			event_target:corrupt_priest_target = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { trait = lustful }
						NOT = { trait = chaste }
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { trait = temperate }
						NOT = { trait = gluttonous }
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { trait = charitable }
						NOT = { trait = greedy }
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { trait = diligent }
						NOT = { trait = slothful }
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { trait = kind }
						OR = {
							NOT = { trait = envious }
							NOT = { trait = cruel }
						}
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { trait = patient }
						NOT = { trait = wroth }
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { trait = humble }
						NOT = { trait = proud }
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { trait = honest }
						NOT = { trait = deceitful }
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { trait = just }
						NOT = { trait = arbitrary }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTOPTA_MNM_7826_TOOLTIP }
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:corrupt_priest_target = {
				character_event = { id = DR_cults.7827 days = 3 random = 27 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_MNM_7826 #remove virtues (slight chance to add new sinful traits)
		trigger = {
			event_target:corrupt_priest_target = {
				OR = {
					trait = chaste
					trait = temperate
					trait = charitable
					trait = diligent
					trait = kind
					trait = patient
					trait = humble
					trait = honest
					trait = just
				}
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTOPTB_MNM_7826_TOOLTIP }
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:corrupt_priest_target = {
				character_event = { id = DR_cults.7828 days = 3 random = 27 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC_MNM_7826 #nevermind I'm a nice guy
		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTOPTC_MNM_7826_TOOLTIP }
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:corrupt_priest_target = {
				clr_character_flag = attempted_corrupt_priest
			}
		}
	}
}

#Ping event for Corrupt a Priest find new sinful traits
character_event = {
	id = DR_cults.7827
	hide_window = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		FROM = { is_devil_worshiper_trigger = yes }
	}

	immediate = {
		event_target:corrupt_priest_target = {
			random_list = {
				10 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						OR = {
							trait = lustful
							trait = chaste
						}
					}
					set_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_lustful
				}
				10 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						OR = {
							trait = gluttonous
							trait = temperate
						}
					}

				}
				10 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						OR = {
							trait = greedy
							trait = charitable
						}
					}
					set_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_greedy
				}
				10 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						OR = {
							trait = slothful
							trait = diligent

					}

						factor = 0
						OR = {
							trait = wroth
							trait = patient

					}

							trait = just
						}
					}
					set_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_arbitrary
				}
				10 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						OR = {
							trait = cruel
							trait = kind
						}
					}
					set_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_cruel
				}
			}
		}
		event_target:corrupt_priest_spell_caster = {
			character_event = { id = DR_cults.7830 }
		}
	}
}

    }

#Ping event for corrupt a priest adding trait successful
character_event = {
	id = DR_cults.7831
	hide_window = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_lustful
			}
			event_target:corrupt_priest_target = {
				add_trait_lustful_effect = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_gluttonous
			}
			event_target:corrupt_priest_target = {
				add_trait_gluttonous_effect = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_greedy
			}
			event_target:corrupt_priest_target = {
				add_trait_greedy_effect = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_slothful
			}
			event_target:corrupt_priest_target = {
				add_trait_slothful_effect = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_envious
			}
			event_target:corrupt_priest_target = {
				add_trait_envious_effect = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_wroth
			}
			event_target:corrupt_priest_target = {
				add_trait_wroth_effect = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_proud
			}
			event_target:corrupt_priest_target = {
				add_trait_proud_effect = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_deceitful
			}
			event_target:corrupt_priest_target = {
				add_trait_deceitful_effect = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_arbitrary
			}
			event_target:corrupt_priest_target = {
				add_trait_arbitrary_effect = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_cruel
			}
			event_target:corrupt_priest_target = {
				add_trait_cruel_effect = yes
			}
		}
		event_target:corrupt_priest_spell_caster = {
			character_event = { id = DR_cults.7832 }
		}
	}
}

            		NOT = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = event_target:corrupt_priest_spell_caster modifier = opinion_successful_corruption } }

    }

    ###bonus descriptions if resulting from event id = DR_cults.7836

    desc = {
        trigger = {
        	event_target:corrupt_priest_target = {
       			AND = {
       				OR = {
       					has_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_lustful
            			has_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_gluttonous
            			has_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_greedy
            			has_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_slothful
            			has_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_envious
            			has_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_wroth
            			has_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_proud
            			has_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_deceitful
            			has_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_arbitrary
            			has_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_cruel
       				}
            		has_opinion_modifier = { who = event_target:corrupt_priest_spell_caster modifier = opinion_successful_corruption }
            	}
            }
        }
        text = EVTDESC_MNM_7832_bonus
    }

	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_MNM_7832 #event option if standard event
		trigger = {
			event_target:corrupt_priest_target = {
				NOT = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = event_target:corrupt_priest_spell_caster modifier = opinion_successful_corruption } }
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTOPTA_MNM_7832_TOOLTIP }
		reverse_opinion = {
			who = event_target:corrupt_priest_target
			modifier = opinion_successful_corruption
			years = 100
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:corrupt_priest_spell_caster = { ai = no }
			}
			event_target:corrupt_priest_target = { set_character_flag = corrupted_by_player }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:corrupt_priest_target = {
				clr_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_lustful
				clr_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_gluttonous
				clr_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_greedy
				clr_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_slothful
				clr_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_envious
				clr_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_wroth
				clr_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_proud
				clr_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_deceitful
				clr_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_arbitrary
				clr_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_cruel
				clr_character_flag = attempted_corrupt_priest
			}
			event_target:corrupt_priest_spell_caster = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NAND = {
							has_quest = quest_devil_worshipers_corrupt_priest
							quest_target = { character = event_target:corrupt_priest_target }
						}
					}
					add_society_currency_minor_effect = yes
				}
				#If quest holder, clear quest and reward
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_quest = quest_devil_worshipers_corrupt_priest
						quest_target = { character = event_target:corrupt_priest_target }
					}
					clr_quest = quest_devil_worshipers_corrupt_priest
					sound_effect = devil_worshippers_corrupt_priest

					if = {
						limit = { event_target:corrupt_priest_target = { higher_tier_than = DUKE } }
						add_society_currency_major_effect = yes
					}
					if = {
						limit = { event_target:corrupt_priest_target = { tier = DUKE } }
						add_society_currency_medium_effect = yes
					}
					if = {
						limit = { event_target:corrupt_priest_target = { lower_tier_than = DUKE } }
						add_society_currency_minor_effect = yes
					}
				}
				minor_chaos_corruption_effect = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_MNM_7832 #event option if bonus event
		trigger = {
			event_target:corrupt_priest_target = {
				has_opinion_modifier = { who = event_target:corrupt_priest_spell_caster modifier = opinion_successful_corruption }
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTOPTB_MNM_7832_TOOLTIP }
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:corrupt_priest_spell_caster = {
				add_society_currency_medium_effect = yes
			}
			event_target:corrupt_priest_target = {
				clr_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_lustful
				clr_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_gluttonous
				clr_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_greedy
				clr_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_slothful
				clr_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_envious
				clr_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_wroth
				clr_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_proud
				clr_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_deceitful
				clr_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_arbitrary
				clr_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_cruel
			}
		}
	}
}

#Corrupt a Priest failed corruption notification
character_event = {
	id = DR_cults.7834
	picture = GFX_evt_scandal
	desc = EVTDESC_MNM_7834
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_MNM_7834
		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTOPTA_MNM_7834_TOOLTIP }
		hidden_effect = {
			increase_visibility_effect = yes
			reverse_opinion = {
				who = event_target:corrupt_priest_target
				modifier = opinion_failed_corruption
				years = 10
			}
			any_realm_character = { #exposed corrupter -10
				opinion = {
					who = event_target:corrupt_priest_spell_caster
					modifier = opinion_known_corrupter
					years = 10
				}
			}
			event_target:corrupt_priest_target = {
				clr_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_lustful
				clr_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_gluttonous
				clr_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_greedy
				clr_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_slothful
				clr_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_envious
				clr_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_wroth
				clr_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_proud
				clr_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_deceitful
				clr_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_arbitrary
				clr_character_flag = corrupt_priest_add_cruel
				clr_character_flag = attempted_corrupt_priest
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_quest = quest_devil_worshipers_corrupt_priest
				}
				clr_quest_target = quest_devil_worshipers_corrupt_priest
			}
		}
	}
}

#Corrupt a priest remove trait: corrupt them!
character_event = {
	id = DR_cults.7835

            	has_character_flag = corrupt_priest_remove_chaste
        	}
        }
        text = EVTDESC_MNM_7835_remove_chaste
    }

            	has_character_flag = corrupt_priest_remove_temperate
        	}

        	event_target:corrupt_priest_target = {
            	has_character_flag = corrupt_priest_remove_charitable

            	has_character_flag = corrupt_priest_remove_humble
        	}
        }
        text = EVTDESC_MNM_7835_remove_humble
    }
    desc = {

        	event_target:corrupt_priest_target = {
            	has_character_flag = corrupt_priest_remove_honest
        	}
        }
        text = EVTDESC_MNM_7835_remove_honest
    }
    desc = {
        trigger = {
        	event_target:corrupt_priest_target = {
            	has_character_flag = corrupt_priest_remove_just
        	}
        }
        text = EVTDESC_MNM_7835_remove_just
    }
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_MNM_7835 #try to corrupt them
		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTOPTA_MNM_7835_TOOLTIP }
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 2
						event_target:corrupt_priest_target = {
							OR = {
								trait = bad_priest_christian
								trait = bad_priest_muslim
								trait = bad_priest_norse
								trait = bad_priest_tengri
								trait = bad_priest_zoroastrian
								trait = bad_priest_aztec
							}
						}
					}
					hidden_effect = {
						event_target:corrupt_priest_target = {
							character_event = { id = DR_cults.7836 days = 15 random = 45 } #success event
						}
					}
				}
				50 = {
					hidden_effect = {
						event_target:corrupt_priest_target = {
							character_event = { id = DR_cults.7833 days = 15 random = 45 } #failure event
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 33
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					diplomacy = 15
					intrigue = 15
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				has_society_currency_minor_trigger = yes
				NAND = {
					has_quest = quest_devil_worshipers_corrupt_priest
					quest_target = { character = event_target:corrupt_priest_target }
				}
			}
		}
		name = EVTOPTB_MNM_7835 #use dark power to corrupt them
		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTOPTB_MNM_7835_TOOLTIP }
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:corrupt_priest_spell_caster = {
				detract_society_currency_minor_effect = yes
			}
			event_target:corrupt_priest_target = {
				character_event = { id = DR_cults.7836 days = 15 random = 45 } #success event
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC_MNM_7835 #use diplomacy to talk them into it
		tooltip_info = diplomacy
		trigger = {
			diplomacy = 15
		}
		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTOPTC_MNM_7835_TOOLTIP }
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				90 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 2
						event_target:corrupt_priest_target = {
							OR = {
								trait = bad_priest_christian
								trait = bad_priest_muslim
								trait = bad_priest_norse
								trait = bad_priest_tengri
								trait = bad_priest_zoroastrian
								trait = bad_priest_aztec
							}
						}
					}
					hidden_effect = {
						event_target:corrupt_priest_target = {
							character_event = { id = DR_cults.7836 days = 15 random = 45 } #success event
						}
					}
				}
				10 = {
					hidden_effect = {
						event_target:corrupt_priest_target = {
							character_event = { id = DR_cults.7833 days = 15 random = 45 } #failure event
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 33
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTD_MNM_7835 #use learning to reason them into it
		tooltip_info = learning
		trigger = {
			learning = 15
		}
		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTOPTD_MNM_7835_TOOLTIP }
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				90 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 2
						event_target:corrupt_priest_target = {
							OR = {
								trait = bad_priest_christian
								trait = bad_priest_muslim
								trait = bad_priest_norse
								trait = bad_priest_tengri
								trait = bad_priest_zoroastrian
								trait = bad_priest_aztec
							}
						}
					}
					hidden_effect = {
						event_target:corrupt_priest_target = {
							character_event = { id = DR_cults.7836 days = 15 random = 45 } #success event
						}
					}

						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 33
		}
	}
